[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer-driven test of `systemctl_parse_argv` triggered an AddressSanitizer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free error in the function `parse_path_argument`. During a fuzzing run, the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msame heap pointer was freed twice: once in `parse_path_argument` and again later [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvia the fuzz harness cleanup, leading to an abort.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzzing of the `systemctl_parse_argv` entry point, AddressSanitizer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected an attempt to free the same memory region two times. This manifests as a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free error in `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msource file [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/shared/parse-argument.c`, line [0m[1;36m68[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, causing the process to abort.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is a double-free vulnerability, which is a form of memory corruption. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDouble freeing a heap allocation can lead to heap metadata corruption, unexpected [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashes, or even potential arbitrary code execution in certain contexts.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important Observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The crash stack trace shows two distinct free operations on the same pointer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m0x502000007310[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - First free in `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m68[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Second free in the fuzz harness cleanup via `static_destruct` in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m74[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The pointer was originally allocated or resized via `realloc` in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_extend_internal` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msource file `src/basic/path-util.c`, line [0m[1;36m585[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, invoked by [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd`, which is called by `parse_path_argument`.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invokes `systemctl_parse_argv` and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafterwards unconditionally calls destructor routines that free all parsed data, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to the second free.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas to Investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To gain a holistic understanding of the root cause, the following components [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be reviewed:  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/shared/parse-argument.c` — the implementation of `parse_path_argument`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mespecially memory allocation and deallocation logic.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/basic/path-util.c` — functions `path_extend_internal` and [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd` to see how buffers are allocated and managed.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/systemctl/fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c` — the fuzz harness, particularly [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe destructor calls in `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` and `static_destruct` to [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand ownership and lifetime expectations.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/systemctl/systemctl.c` — the `systemctl_parse_argv` wrapper to track how [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed arguments are collected and later freed.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
